15 Mirror Coat - Psychic
15 Safeguard - Normal Unique Traits - Weeble
Wobbufett are very limited when it comes to
their Move variety. As a result, Wobbufett can use
Counter and Mirror Coat as EOT Frequency
Moves rather than as Battle Frequency Moves.
However, after the first use of Mirror Coat or
Counter during an encounter, meaning on the
second use of Mirror Coat or the second use of
Counter and from that point on during the
encounter, Wobbufett’s Defense and Special
Defense are treated as if they are ten less (-10).
This penalty is only active while calculating
damage and while using Mirror Coat and Counter
after the first use per Encounter. If a PP Up is used
on a Wobbufett’s Counter or Mirror Coat,
Weeble is not needed for that Move anymore.

roll 1d4 and 1d20. For the 1d4 roll, a result of
1 makes the Damage Dice Roll 2d10; a result of
2 makes the Damage Dice Roll 4d6; a result of 3
makes the Damage Dice Roll 3d10; a result of 4
makes the Damage Dice Roll 2d20. For the 1d20
roll, the Type is Bug on a result of 1; Dark on 2;
Dragon on 3; Electric on 4; Fighting on 5; Fire on
6; Flying on 7; Ghost on 8; Grass on 9; Ground on
10; Ice on 11; Normal on 12; Poison on 13;
Psychic on 14; Rock on 15; Steel on 16; Water on
17; and on a result of 18-20, reroll the d20. Those
become the permanent stats of Hidden Power.
Capture Rate: 25
Experience Drop: 5
